Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

	output out

	input areset,
	output out

Task fsm3 passed.
Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

Task fsm3 passed.
Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	reg [1:0] state;
	reg [1:0] next_state;
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	
	always @(*) begin
		case(state)
			A: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			B: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			C: begin
				if(in) next_state <= D;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			D: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			default: next_state <= A;
		endcase
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk or posedge areset) begin
		if(areset) state <= A;
		else state <= next_state;
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D);
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
); 
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
); 
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	reg [1:0] state;
	reg [1:0] next_state;
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	
	always @(*) begin
		case(state)
			A: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			B: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			C: begin
				if(in) next_state <= D;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			D: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			default: next_state <= A;
		endcase
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk or posedge areset) begin
		if(areset) state <= A;
		else state <= next_state;
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D);
	
endmodule

Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
); 
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	reg [1:0] state;
	reg [1:0] next_state;
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	
	always @(*) begin
		case(state)
			A: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			B: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			C: begin
				if(in) next_state <= D;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			D: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			default: next_state <= A;
		endcase
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk or posedge areset) begin
		if(areset) state <= A;
		else state <= next_state;
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D);
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end

					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;

Task fsm3 passed.
Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

Task fsm3 passed.
Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	reg [1:0] state;
	reg [1:0] next_state;
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	
	always @(*) begin
		case(state)
			A: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			B: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			C: begin
				if(in) next_state <= D;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			D: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			default: next_state <= A;
		endcase
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk or posedge areset) begin
		if(areset) state <= A;
		else state <= next_state;
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D);
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);    
    
    parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
    reg [1:0] state, next_state;
    
    always @(*) begin
        state <= next_state;
    end
    
    always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
        if(areset)
            next_state <= A;
        else
            begin
                case(state)
                    A: begin
                        if(in)
                            next_state <= B;
                        else
                            next_state <= A;
                    end
                    B: begin
                        if(in)
                            next_state <= B;
                        else
                            next_state <= C;

                        if(in)

                        else
                            next_state <= A;

                        if(in)
                            next_state <= B;
                        else
                            next_state <= C;
                    end
                    default: begin
                        next_state <= A;
                    end
                endcase
            end
    end

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end

					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A = 0, B = 1, C = 2, D = 3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end

					else

				end

					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);    
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end

		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else

						next_state <= B;
					else

					else
						next_state <= C;
				end

			endcase
	end

// A | A, B | 0

// C | A, D | 0

module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;

		state <= next_state;

				end

Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	reg [1:0] state;
	reg [1:0] next_state;
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	
	always @(*) begin
		case(state)
			A: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			B: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			C: begin
				if(in) next_state <= D;
				else next_state <= A;
			end
			D: begin
				if(in) next_state <= B;
				else next_state <= C;
			end
			default: next_state <= A;
		endcase
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk or posedge areset) begin
		if(areset) state <= A;
		else state <= next_state;
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D);
	
endmodule

Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

Task fsm3 passed.
Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);    
    
    parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
    reg [1:0] state, next_state;
    
    always @(*) begin
        state <= next_state;
    end
    
    always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
        if(areset)
            next_state <= A;
        else
            begin
                case(state)
                    A: begin
                        if(in)
                            next_state <= B;
                        else
                            next_state <= A;
                    end
                    B: begin
                        if(in)
                            next_state <= B;
                        else
                            next_state <= C;
                    end
                    C: begin
                        if(in)
                            next_state <= D;
                        else
                            next_state <= A;
                    end
                    D: begin
                        if(in)
                            next_state <= B;
                        else
                            next_state <= C;
                    end
                    default: begin
                        next_state <= A;
                    end
                endcase
            end
    end
    
    assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
    
endmodule

// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
); 
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out

Terminal state:  The following is the state transition table for a Moore state machine with one input, one output, and four states. Implement this state machine. Include a positive edge triggered asynchronous reset that resets the FSM to state A.
 
// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);

	parameter A = 0, B = 1, C = 2, D = 3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

// state | next state in=0, next state in=1 | output
// A | A, B | 0
// B | C, B | 0
// C | A, D | 0
// D | C, B | 1
module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
	reg [1:0] state, next_state;
	
	always @(*) begin
		state <= next_state;
	end
	
	always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
		if(areset)
			next_state <= A;
		else
			case(state)
				A: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				B: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				C: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= D;
					else
						next_state <= A;
				end
				D: begin
					if(in)
						next_state <= B;
					else
						next_state <= C;
				end
				default: next_state <= A;
			endcase
	end
	
	assign out = (state == D)? 1:0;
	
endmodule

// A | A, B | 0

module top_module (
	input clk,
	input in,
	input areset,
	output out
);
	
	parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
